We continue to view FT’s risk reward profile as unattractive pending the outcome of strategy review
Although we see significant scope for FT to cut costs and deliver compelling yield and even though the CEO has strong track record execution the government role in giving FT the flexibility it requires is pivotal
In the meantime liquidity risk remains and in our view right issue is matter of when not if The government’s role will again be pivotal in refinancing and reducing this debt However it is liquidity or refinancing risk that is the nearterm focus of FT and rating agencies alike with daunting refinancing schedule ahead in This would be impossible without government intervention even FT acknowledged this in its conference call subrayado

NERA cociente endeudamiento define relación deuda plazo conjunto recursos plazo deuda capital The debt ratio is defined as the ratio of long term debt to long term capital debt and equity
NERA relación deuda capital social calcula relación deuda plazo capital The debtequity ratio is calculated as the ratio of longterm debt to equity
NERA timesinterestearned ratio interest cover indica medida intereses cubiertos resultado intereses impuestos amortizaciones EBIT medida indica nivel adecuación flujo caja generado empresa aptitud frente pago intereses
the timesinterestearned ratio or interest cover measures the extent to which interest is covered by earnings before interest and taxes ENIT plus depreciation The measure gives level of the adequacy of cash flow generation and the consequent comfort company enjoys in meeting its interest payments
NERA cálculos basan datos proporcionados FT estimaciones cubren intereses principal vinculados empréstitos obligacionistas bonos tesorería intereses bonos tesorería tuvieron julio diciembre inexistencia datos fechas anteriores Calculations based on data supplied by France Telecom
Figures include bond and commercial paper interest and principal interest on commercial paper was computed from July to December due to data unavailability for previous dates
inversores utilizan credit ratings indicadores probabilidad obtener reembolso conforme términos regulan inversión calificaciones crediticias denominación rango inversión categorías internacionalmente incluidas AAA BBB plazo corto plazo indican probabilidad relativamente baja incumplimiento calificaciones categorías especulativas rango inversión internacionalmente BB plazo corto plazo indicar elevada probabilidad incumplimiento producido incumplimiento sitio Internet Fitchs Rating httpwwwfitchratingscom
Credit ratings are used by investors as indications of the likelihood of repayment in accordance with the terms on which they invested Thus the use of credit ratings defines their function investment grade ratings international longterm AAA BBB categories shortterm indicate relatively low probability of default while those in the speculative or noninvestment grade categories international longterm BB shortterm may signal higher probability of default or that default has already occurred sitio Internet Fitchs Rating httpwwwfitchratingscom

destacó NERA economistas teóricos estudiaron minuciosamente importancia valor reputación prácticamente relaciones económicas incertidumbre naturaleza mayoría casos interviene serie transacciones similares período determinado corriente ambas partes intenten hacerse reputación pudiera beneficiarles fase posterior
años economistas estudiado rigor fenómeno adquiere reputación número publicaciones revistas especializadas sustancial Abundan aplicaciones concepto básico distintos ámbitos limitamos ejemplos actividades bancos centrales organización industrial mercados deuda soberana
establecerse reputación importante ámbito préstamo empréstito escala internacional entidad soberana deudor privado incumple obligación reembolsar préstamo dificultades atraer fuentes crédito sucesivo
parecen preferir retroceso económico dificultades implica situación suspensión pagos sentido Gobierno francés gobierno cumple compromisos asumidos función administrador numerosas empresas comerciales negocios afectan posición fiscal palabra careciese crédito ámbitos resultaría costoso economists and game theorists have studied extensively the importance and value of reputation In almost any economic relationship there is some degree of uncertainty regarding the nature of the counter party However very often party is involved in not single but whole series of similar transactions over period of time It is common observation that one or both parties may seek to establish reputation for themselves as this may be beneficial later on
David Kreps and Robert Wilson Reputation and Imperfect Information JOURNAL OF ECONOMIC THEORY ‘Economists have studied the phenomenon of reputation acquisition rigorously over the past years and the list of publications in leading journals is sizeable
The acquisition of reputation is also important in the area of international borrowing and lending
Jeremy Bulow and Kenneth Rogoff overeign Debt Is to Forgive to Forget AMERICAN ECONOMIC REVIEW In the same vein the French government benefits from reputation for honouring the commitment it makes regarding its management of many commercial enterprises and matters affecting the fiscal position of the government
It would be very costly if its word could not be believed in these matters

on July downgraded France Télécom’s ratings to BBB The agency longer expects France Télécom to hit the net debt EBITDA target by but did assign stable outlook to the low triple ratings It seems that the stable outlook is anchored by the French state which has clearly indicated to Standard Poor’s that it will behave as an aware investor and would take appropriate steps if France Télécom were to face any difficulties Interestingly had initially said it was not incorporating any extraordinary support from the French government into its rating when it downgraded France Télécom’s ratings to BBB in June Since then the agency appears to have taken an about face in stating that the conclusions of the creditwatch status follows an analysis of the company’s liquidity position through the end of and review of the French state’s potential involvement in the French telecommunications market France Télécom benefited from the market’s increased confidence that the French government will in one way or another support the credit we cannot ignore the fact that FT is majority owned by the French State and recent comments from the French finance Ministry have reassured investor that liquidity will be provided page However as we have consistently mentioned we expect that the company will ultimately find all the liquidity it needs via the socalled implicit government support This could take the form of banks or the government providing the necessary loans at market prices
obstante what is the market price for say bn of new debt to BBB credit
we suspect there is right answer to these questions because if FT was operating in the real world it would not be able to refinance without debt for equity swap in our view ”p
